  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_b67335ee-b29f-4181-bb2b-34568be493fd'

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer934967379" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3908959154294882816"><strong>Enjoyably Witchy </strong><br/><br/>A good ending for an enjoyable series. The characters are likeable, and there's plenty of action and magic. The other books in the series all ended in cliffhangers. Not this one though, it wrapped everything up nicely. If you enjoy witch stories, I recommend these. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_1148714864" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1148714864" />
    <a title="Kriselda Gray" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8603151-kriselda-gray"><img alt="Kriselda Gray" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1495384084p2/8603151.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1148714864?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kriselda Gray" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kriselda Gray" href="/user/show/8603151-kriselda-gray">Kriselda Gray</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18902019-all-hallows-eve">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1148714864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15414896515128028545"><strong>Beautiful finale to a good series</strong><br/><br/>When I started the first book of "The New England Witch Chronicles" I wasn't sure I was going to like it, but I decided to give it at least 3 or 4 chapters before I made up my mind because something in the first few pages made me think it might be worthwhile. I'm really glad I did, as the series turned out to be quite good. Each book was stronger than the one before it, and there was enough tension to keep it interesting without it being overwhelming. Alexandria </span>
  <span id="freeText15414896515128028545" style="display:none"><strong>Beautiful finale to a good series</strong><br /><br />When I started the first book of "The New England Witch Chronicles" I wasn't sure I was going to like it, but I decided to give it at least 3 or 4 chapters before I made up my mind because something in the first few pages made me think it might be worthwhile. I'm really glad I did, as the series turned out to be quite good. Each book was stronger than the one before it, and there was enough tension to keep it interesting without it being overwhelming. Alexandria Ramsay is a likable, believable heroine and the book allows for plenty of time for a nice, solid non-instaromance to blossom and grow, friendships to be formed and friendships to fade - all in-between her battles with the forces of evil. While there's little doubt as to the outcome of the final battle, there is a twist to it, and the series closes with a touching epilogue. If you like witchy fiction, this is a good, solid story that I expect you'll enjoy.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15414896515128028545" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I really did! Now I'm just sitting here feeling lost because the series is over, and I'm not sure I'm ready to let it go!</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/604339620" />
    <a title="Allison Landers" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6853180-allison-landers"><img alt="Allison Landers" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1480807477p2/6853180.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/604339620?book_show_action=true">May 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison Landers" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison Landers" href="/user/show/6853180-allison-landers">Allison Landers</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6853180-allison-landers?shelf=kickass">kickass</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer604339620" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9049122144202889355">Ahhh maybe 4.5? I don't know it was awesome and I read it really fast, but I couldn't quite give it 5 stars just because the epilogue felt really abrupt to me after what had just happened... And I still don't know how I feel about it. But, overall this book was great! I loved the whole series! Alex is awesome and did awesome kickass witchy things and it was so much fun. I think these are going on the re-read list!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer13304591727490793329">Chelse Bellingeri has done it again! This is the final installment of the New England Witch Chronicles, and it was AMAZING! Keep writing, Chelsea!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('J0V2cGOynHJDZl7kvxJ4UGAFWh8uYpZen1Ky3bMlgbUT8GFHMWcjjloiZa8mcIg5b3Pdy6Eg5HAFyG/Qd4C93A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UJQ5oUcBimE4pNJyr1JUdKW1BlnV/NYkSh+2qbGursdkIS6WFdQ1nSHg6Tk2MKQdqsOBjVq+pArQhWukdQuSrg==')})
  }

      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_7011653'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7011653-daughters-of-the-witching-hill?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Daughters of the Witching Hill<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/45115.Mary_Sharratt?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Mary Sharratt<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p6\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p0\"><\/span><\/span> 3.73 avg rating &mdash; 4,440 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2010\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer13679090692414409112\">Daughters of the Witching Hill brings history to life in a vivid and wrenching account of a family sustained by love as they try to survive the hysteria of a witch-hunt. Bess Southerns, an impoverished widow living in Pendle Forest, is haunted by vis<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText13679090692414409112\" style=\"display:none\">Daughters of the Witching Hill brings history to life in a vivid and wrenching account of a family sustained by love as they try to survive the hysteria of a witch-hunt. Bess Southerns, an impoverished widow living in Pendle Forest, is haunted by visions and gains a reputation as a cunning woman. Drawing on the Catholic folk magic of her youth, Bess heals the sick and foretells the future. As she ages, she instructs her granddaughter, Alizon, in her craft, as well as her best friend, who ultimately turns to dark magic. When a peddler suffers a stroke after exchanging harsh words with Alizon, a local magistrate, eager to make his name as a witch finder, plays neighbors and family members against one another until suspicion and paranoia reach frenzied heights. Sharratt interweaves well-researched historical details of the 1612 Pendle witch-hunt with a beautifully imagined story of strong women, family, and betrayal. Daughters of the Witching Hill is a powerful novel of intrigue and revelation.<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"13679090692414409112\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return <span id="freeTextContainer6566457960893340918">Chelsea Luna is the author of the bestselling NEW ENGLAND WITCH CHRONICLES, a young adult paranormal romance series comprising of four novels.   <span id="freeText6566457960893340918" style="display:none">Chelsea Luna is the author of the bestselling NEW ENGLAND WITCH CHRONICLES, a young adult paranormal romance series comprising of four novels.
